66	_EPHEMERIS_NOTE = """You can either give an explicit ephemeris or use a default, which is normally
67	    a built-in ephemeris that does not require ephemeris files.  To change
68	    the default to be the JPL ephemeris::
69	
70	        >>> from astropy.coordinates import solar_system_ephemeris
71	        >>> solar_system_ephemeris.set('jpl')  # doctest: +SKIP
72	
73	    Use of any JPL ephemeris requires the jplephem package
74	    (https://pypi.org/project/jplephem/).
75	    If needed, the ephemeris file will be downloaded (and cached).
76	
77	    One can check which bodies are covered by a given ephemeris using::
78	
79	        >>> solar_system_ephemeris.bodies
80	        ('earth', 'sun', 'moon', 'mercury', 'venus', 'earth-moon-barycenter', 'mars', 'jupiter', 'saturn', 'uranus', 'neptune')"""

1	READ_DOCSTRING = """
2	    Read the input ``table`` and return the table.  Most of the default behavior for
3	    various parameters is determined by the ``format`` argument.
4	
5	    Help on the ``read()`` function arguments is available as shown in this example::
6	
7	      from astropy.io import ascii
8	      ascii.read.help()  # Common help for all formats
9	      ascii.read.help("html")  # Common help plus "html" format-specific args
10	
11	    See also:
12	
13	    - https://docs.astropy.org/en/stable/io/ascii/
14	    - https://docs.astropy.org/en/stable/io/ascii/read.html
15	
16	    Parameters
17	    ----------
18	    table : str, file-like, list, `pathlib.Path` object
19	        Input table as a file name, file-like object, list of string[s],
20	        single newline-separated string or `pathlib.Path` object.
21	    guess : bool
22	        Try to guess the table format. Defaults to None.
23	    format : str, `~astropy.io.ascii.BaseReader`
24	        Input table format
25	    delimiter : str
26	        Column delimiter string
27	    comment : str
28	        Regular expression defining a comment line in table
29	    quotechar : str
30	        One-character string to quote fields containing special characters
31	    header_start : int
32	        Line index for the header line not counting comment or blank lines.
33	        A line with only whitespace is considered blank.
34	    data_start : int
35	        Line index for the start of data not counting comment or blank lines.
36	        A line with only whitespace is considered blank.
37	    data_end : int
38	        Line index for the end of data not counting comment or blank lines.
39	        This value can be negative to count from the end.
40	    converters : dict
41	        Dictionary of converters to specify output column dtypes. Each key in
42	        the dictionary is a column name or else a name matching pattern
43	        including wildcards. The value is either a data type such as ``int`` or
44	        ``np.float32``; a list of such types which is tried in order until a
45	        successful conversion is achieved; or a list of converter tuples (see
46	        the `~astropy.io.ascii.convert_numpy` function for details).
47	    names : list
48	        List of names corresponding to each data column
49	    include_names : list
50	        List of names to include in output.
51	    exclude_names : list
52	        List of names to exclude from output (applied after ``include_names``)
53	    fill_values : tuple, list of tuple
54	        specification of fill values for bad or missing table values
55	    fill_include_names : list
56	        List of names to include in fill_values.
57	    fill_exclude_names : list
58	        List of names to exclude from fill_values (applied after ``fill_include_names``)
59	    fast_reader : bool, str or dict
60	        Whether to use the C engine, can also be a dict with options which
61	        defaults to `False`; parameters for options dict:
62	
63	        use_fast_converter: bool
64	            enable faster but slightly imprecise floating point conversion method
65	        exponent_style: str
66	            One-character string defining the exponent or ``'Fortran'`` to auto-detect
67	            Fortran-style scientific notation like ``'3.14159D+00'`` (``'E'``, ``'D'``, ``'Q'``),
68	            all case-insensitive; default ``'E'``, all other imply ``use_fast_converter``
69	        chunk_size : int
70	            If supplied with a value > 0 then read the table in chunks of
71	            approximately ``chunk_size`` bytes. Default is reading table in one pass.
72	        chunk_generator : bool
73	            If True and ``chunk_size > 0`` then return an iterator that returns a
74	            table for each chunk.  The default is to return a single stacked table
75	            for all the chunks.
76	
77	    encoding : str
78	        Allow to specify encoding to read the file (default= ``None``).
79	
80	    Other Parameters
81	    ----------------
82	    inputter_cls : `~astropy.io.ascii.BaseInputter`
83	        Inputter class
84	    outputter_cls : `~astropy.io.ascii.BaseOutputter`
85	        Outputter class
86	    data_splitter_cls : `~astropy.io.ascii.BaseSplitter`
87	        Splitter class to split data columns
88	    header_splitter_cls : `~astropy.io.ascii.BaseSplitter`
89	        Splitter class to split header columns
90	
91	    Returns
92	    -------
93	    dat : `~astropy.table.Table` or <generator>
94	        Output table
95	
96	    """

>> Issue: [B824:url_found] url_found
   Severity: Medium   Confidence: Medium
   Location: /home/blue/PyPIAgent/Dataset/study/unzip_benign/astropy-7.0.1/astropy-7.0.1/astropy/nddata/mixins/ndarithmetic.py:20
   More Info: https://bandit.readthedocs.io/en/latest/plugins/b824_url_found.html
19	# Docstring templates for add, subtract, multiply, divide methods.
20	_arit_doc = """
21	    Performs {name} by evaluating ``self`` {op} ``operand``.
22	
23	    Parameters
24	    ----------
25	    operand, operand2 : `NDData`-like instance
26	        If ``operand2`` is ``None`` or not given it will perform the operation
27	        ``self`` {op} ``operand``.
28	        If ``operand2`` is given it will perform ``operand`` {op} ``operand2``.
29	        If the method was called on a class rather than on the instance
30	        ``operand2`` must be given.
31	
32	    propagate_uncertainties : `bool` or ``None``, optional
33	        If ``None`` the result will have no uncertainty. If ``False`` the
34	        result will have a copied version of the first operand that has an
35	        uncertainty. If ``True`` the result will have a correctly propagated
36	        uncertainty from the uncertainties of the operands but this assumes
37	        that the uncertainties are `NDUncertainty`-like. Default is ``True``.
38	
39	        .. versionchanged:: 1.2
40	            This parameter must be given as keyword-parameter. Using it as
41	            positional parameter is deprecated.
42	            ``None`` was added as valid parameter value.
43	
44	    handle_mask : callable, ``'first_found'`` or ``None``, optional
45	        If ``None`` the result will have no mask. If ``'first_found'`` the
46	        result will have a copied version of the first operand that has a
47	        mask). If it is a callable then the specified callable must
48	        create the results ``mask`` and if necessary provide a copy.
49	        Default is `numpy.logical_or`.
50	
51	        .. versionadded:: 1.2
52	
53	    handle_meta : callable, ``'first_found'`` or ``None``, optional
54	        If ``None`` the result will have no meta. If ``'first_found'`` the
55	        result will have a copied version of the first operand that has a
56	        (not empty) meta. If it is a callable then the specified callable must
57	        create the results ``meta`` and if necessary provide a copy.
58	        Default is ``None``.
59	
60	        .. versionadded:: 1.2
61	
62	    compare_wcs : callable, ``'first_found'`` or ``None``, optional
63	        If ``None`` the result will have no wcs and no comparison between
64	        the wcs of the operands is made. If ``'first_found'`` the
65	        result will have a copied version of the first operand that has a
66	        wcs. If it is a callable then the specified callable must
67	        compare the ``wcs``. The resulting ``wcs`` will be like if ``False``
68	        was given otherwise it raises a ``ValueError`` if the comparison was
69	        not successful. Default is ``'first_found'``.
70	
71	        .. versionadded:: 1.2
72	
73	    uncertainty_correlation : number or `~numpy.ndarray`, optional
74	        The correlation between the two operands is used for correct error
75	        propagation for correlated data as given in:
76	        https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Propagation_of_uncertainty#Example_formulas
77	        Default is 0.
78	
79	        .. versionadded:: 1.2
80	
81	
82	    kwargs :
83	        Any other parameter that should be passed to the callables used.
84	
85	    Returns
86	    -------
87	    result : `~astropy.nddata.NDData`-like
88	        The resulting dataset
89	
90	    Notes
91	    -----
92	    If a ``callable`` is used for ``mask``, ``wcs`` or ``meta`` the
93	    callable must accept the corresponding attributes as first two
94	    parameters. If the callable also needs additional parameters these can be
95	    defined as ``kwargs`` and must start with ``"wcs_"`` (for wcs callable) or
96	    ``"meta_"`` (for meta callable). This startstring is removed before the
97	    callable is called.
98	
99	    ``"first_found"`` can also be abbreviated with ``"ff"``.
100	    """
101

103	class NDArithmeticMixin:
